[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer-detected dynamic stack buffer overflow occurred in the AVIF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary’s YUV-to-RGB conversion code. The overflow was triggered by the fuzzing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness `YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` when calling the slow conversion path [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`. The crash arises from a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read beyond a stack [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer in `reformat.c` at line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A stack-based buffer overflow was detected by AddressSanitizer in the function [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` within `src/libavif/src/reformat.c`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow manifests as a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read past the end of a stack-allocated buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mAddressSanitizer reports “Left alloca redzone”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability type:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Dynamic stack buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstack-based[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mObservations and findings:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash occurs deep in the YUV→RGB slow conversion routine, specifically at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`reformat.[0m[1;92mc:812:46[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb@YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m drives the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode by creating an `avifImage` instance and invoking `avifImageYUVToRGB`, which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls the slow path under certain conditions.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow address lies in the red zone of an `alloca`-ed buffer, indicating an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder-sized or miscalculated stack allocation.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The backtrace shows the chain: `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` → [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVToRGBImpl` → `avifImageYUVToRGB` → the fuzz test’s `Convert` helper.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode areas for investigation:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The implementation of `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` in `reformat.c`, especially [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maround line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m where the overflow was detected. Check how the stack buffer is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msized and how pixel or channel indexes are computed.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Related conversion logic in `avifImageYUVToRGBImpl` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1713[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic wrapper `avifImageYUVToRGB` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1844[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzz test helper `Convert` in `tests/gtest/avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb.cc` to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand which parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage dimensions, chroma sampling choices, boolean [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m may lead into the slow conversion path and trigger the buffer misuse.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m818[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m   [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Investigate and Confirm Root Cause[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buffers `uspill_image` and `vspill_image` are declared as VLA arrays of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdimensions `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m673[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Valid indices are `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m ≤ x < width` for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe first index and `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m ≤ y < height` for the second.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the “spill dampening” branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m807[0m[39m and neighbor updates at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m810[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m818[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code computes signed offsets `a` and `b` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m based on parity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes **no bounds checking** before using them to index `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, etc.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `i` or `j` is zero [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor at the maximum index[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `i+a` or `j+b` underflows [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor overflows, producing an out-of-bounds access and thus the [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer-detected stack overflow.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parity-based dampening concept [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapplying small subtractions to the four [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiagonal neighbors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is crucial to the algorithm.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The main spill-distribution loop already uses a similar scheme of [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`adjCol`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`adjRow` with bounds checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m786[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m794[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Reuse that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern in the dampening branch to keep behavior consistent.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/reformat.c`, locate the dampening branch beginning at line ~[0m[1;36m798[0m[39m:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m0x1000[0m[39m && total_spill > [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          int a = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          int b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m *** Insert bounds-clamp here for a and b ***[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[33m...[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m     -= pSpillCb;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m     -= pSpillCr;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m also correct likely typo here[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCb;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCr;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCb;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCr;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after computing `a` and `b`, add:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clamp horizontal offset to stay within [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, width[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + a < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + a >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clamp vertical offset to stay within [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, height[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + b < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + b >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Fix the apparent typo on line [0m[1;36m811[0m[39m: [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` should subtract `pSpillCr`, not `pSpillCb`.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Eliminates the overflow** by ensuring `i+a` and `j+b` always lie in the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid index range before any access.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirrors the existing, tested neighbor-clamping approach used earlier in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`adjCol`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`adjRow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preserving the dampening algorithm’s intent.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does **not** alter harness or test code, nor external dependencies; keeps all [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting fuzzer inputs and behaviors unchanged.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Correctly handles underflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen `i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `a == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`i == width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` and `a == +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for both dimensions.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side effects are minimal: at image borders, dampening will only apply to the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcenter pixel [0m[1;39m([0m[39msince off-image offsets are zeroed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is acceptable and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistent with earlier boundary code.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Code Ranges to Patch[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m807[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Post-Patch Validation[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild and run the existing fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m under [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer; the dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow should no longer trigger.[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally, add a small unit test targeting a tiny [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m image to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure border dampening logic behaves without OOB.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
